    print(num*s)

while True:
    try:
        b = float(input("enter base - "))
        h = float(input("enter height - "))
    except:
        print("valid number")
    else:
        area = (b*h)/2
        print(area)
        break

# Write a Python program to sum of three given integers. However, if two values are equal sum will be zero. 
while True:
    try:
        a = int(input(" 1st number - "))
        b = int(input(" 2nd number - "))
        c = int(input("3rd number - "))
    except:
        print("enter valid number")
    else:
        if (a==b) or (b==c) or (c==a):
            print("0")
            break
        else:
            print(a+b+c)
            break

# 34. Write a Python program to sum of two given integers. However, if the sum is between 15 to 20 it will return 20. Go to the editor
# Click me to see the sample solution

while True:
    try:
        a = int(input(" enter 1st number - "))
        b = int(input("enter 2nd number - "))
    except:
        print("enter valid number")
    else:
        if 15 <=(a+b) <=20:
            print("20")
            break

while True:
    try:
        a = int(input("enter 1st number - "))
        b = int(input("enter 2nd numbver - "))
    except:
        print("enter valid number - ")
    else:
        if a==b or a+b == 5 or a-b == 5:
            print("true")
            break
        else:
            break

# Write a Python program to add two objects if both objects are an integer type

while True:
    try:
        a = int(input("enter 1st number"))
        b = int(input("enter 2nd number"))
    except:
        print("enter valid number")
    else:
        if type(a) == int and type(b) == int:
            print(a+b)
            break
        else:
            print("useless")
            break

def cross(x,y):
    a = x**2+y**2+2*x*y
    return a

In [21]:
# Write a python program to find the sum of the first n positive integers.

def ss (n):
    total = 0
    m = 0
    while m<=n:
        total = total+m
        m = m+1
    return total

import socket

mysock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)                 

mysock.connect(("www.py4inf.com" , 80))
mysock.send(b'GET /code/romeo.txt HTTP/1.0\r\nHost: www.py4inf.com\r\n\r\n')

while True:
    data = mysock.recv(512)
    if ( len(data) < 1 ) :
        break
    print(data)
mysock.close()

# Write a Python program to calculate the sum of the digits in an integer.
while True:
    try:
        a =(input("enter number - "))
    except:
        print("entervalid number - ")
    else:
        b = list(a)
        i = 0
        total = 0
        while i < len(b):
            total = total+int(b[i])
            i = i+1
        print(total)
        break
            
        

enter number - 111
3

# Write a Python program to sort three integers without using conditional statements and loops.
a = int(input("enter 1stnumber - "))
b = int(input("enter 2nd number - "))
c = int(input("enter 3rd number - "))
lst = []
lst.append(a)
lst.append(b)
lst.append(c)
lst.sort()

enter 2nd number - 0
enter 3rd number - 4

    self.age = age

p1.myfunc()

# Define a function number_of_lines
# Open the file mbox-short.txt which is located at /cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt
# Read the file into one string by using read method on file handle
# Write logic to count the number of lines
# Return the count of the number of lines
# PS - If your logic is correct then your function should return 1910. You can use "Hint" and "See Answer" if you are stuck.
In [29]:
def number_of_lines():
    hand = open('/cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt')
    nxt = hand.read()
    Counter = 0
    CoList = nxt.split("\n") 
  
    for i in CoList: 
        if i: 
            Counter += 1
          
    print("This is the number of lines in the file") 
    print(Counter)

def number_of_lines():
    hand = open('/cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt')
    file = hand.read()
    count = 0
    new = file.split('\n')
    for i in new:
        if i:
            count = count+1
    print(count)

Define a function average_spam_confidence which calculates the average spam confidence and returns it
Open the file mbox-short.txt which is located at /cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt
Loop through the file handle
Select only those lines starts with X-DSPAM-Confidence:
Split the lines at : and take the float value which is spam confidence
Find the average of this spam confidence in the entire file and return it.
In [47]:
def average_spam_confidence():
    fhand = open('/cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt')
    sum = 0
    count = 0
    for line in fhand:
        line = line.rstrip()
        if line.startswith("X-DSPAM-Confidence"):
            char,val = line.split(":")
            sum = sum + float(val)
            count = count+1
    return sum/count

def find_email_sent_days():
    fhand = open('/cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt')
    dct = {}
    lst = []
    for line in fhand:
        line = line.rstrip()
        if line.startswith('From') and len(line) > 3:
            lst = line.split(' ')
            lst.append(lst[2])
            print(lst)

In [ ]:
def find_email_sent_days():
    daysdict = {}
    dayslist = []

    with open("/cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt") as f:
        for line in f:
            dayslist = line.split()
            if len(dayslist) > 3 and line.startswith('From'):
                day = dayslist[2]
                if day not in daysdict:
                    daysdict[day] = 1
                else:
                    daysdict[day] += 1
    return daysdict

def find_email_sent_days():
    f = open('/cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt')

    for line in f:

        if line.startswith('From') and len(line) > 3:
            day = lst[2]
            if day not in dct:
                dct[day] = 1
            else:
                dct[day] = dct[day] + 1
    return dct

In [32]:
def count_message_from_email():
    lineslist=[]
    emaildict={}
    with open("/cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt") as f:
      for line in f:
        lineslist = line.split()
        if line.startswith('From:'):
          email=lineslist[1]
          if email not in emaildict:
            emaildict[email] = 1
          else:
            emaildict[email] += 1
    return emaildict

In [43]:
def count_message_from_domain():
    f = open('/cxldata/datasets/project/mbox-short.txt')
    lst = []
    dct = {}
    for line in f:
        lst = line.split()
        if "@" in line and line.startswith('From:'):
            key = line[line.find("@")+1:].split()[0]
            if key in dct:
                dct[key] = dct[key]+1
            else:
                dct[key] = 1
    return dct

lst = [1,2,3,4,7]
i = 0
for j in lst:
    while i < len(lst):
        mult = j*lst[i+1]
        i = i+1
        if mult%2 != 0:
            print("False",j,lst[i])
        else:
            print("true")
